Story:N/A
Message:Here is a semi-complete (I say this because I'm positive there are other places) list of food establishments we must, as the youth profess, "hit up" during my time back in the States. While it is not necessary to exhaust this list I would like to "hit up" as many as possible so that I may look back upon this time and believe wholeheartedly that the 10 lbs I will inevitably gain from these adventures were, in fact, worth it. 

Watt's 
Merritt's 
La Farm 
Coquette 
BUFFALO WILD WINGS
Dame's 
Cafe Beyu (if only for a nostalgic drink)
Five Guys 
Med Deli
Founding Farmers (come to DC)
The lobstah truck (see above) 
Shiki (to kill this craving for American sushi)
Sugarland for a martini (nobody drives for three hours afterwards)
Lantern (for another nostalgic drink)
Irregardless Cafe 
Allen & Sons 

Please add to this list as you see fit. Upon hitting the tender age of 23 I can no longer ingest caffeine without disastrous side effects and I am sure that even the capabilities of my memory have been affected by the epidemic of "old age."

Name:How to drive object attributes in Maya with music-sound (Tutorial)
Story:N/A
Message:I think we should all watch this video asap.

Our work may be partially cut out for us. Of course, we could always work to make the visualization more pretty or awesome (grapes). But it looks like this might take care of the foundations once and for all.

Incidentally, the "audiowave" node's only output-modifying attribute is "Scale". It looks like this is just a simple output scaling factor. Ideally, though, we'd have a full DFT breakdown, and we could control output not just by modifying scale, but also by restricting the amplitude readout to particular bands of frequency, etc. Ideally, we could select bands and then output a single scaled amplitude readout for each of these bands.

Anyway, though, this is a big deal. That would be awesome if we could get the audiowave source code, though I doubt it.

Message:International outlook 

 Our portfolio is looking to avoid the Japanese economy as the latest quarter GDP results reveal the anaemic growth that the country is experiencing. We are doubtful that the stimulus package the Bank of Japan is administering will yield much result as companies are holding onto low inventory levels. Similarly the Australian economy is looking stagnant with no new information being reported by the Reserve Bank of Australia. The Aussie saw a peculiar increase than immediate decrease of from 93 US cents to 92.69 by statements released to the public. As the Australian economy seems uncertain with its direction our portfolio is also to avoid this sector.

Story:N/A
Message:Hey so what I think I'm going to do for my portion is expect as input 3 integers that sum to 32 (they will be bass, mid-range, treble passed in that order) so I'll figure out how to aggregate the ranges.  Then I'll expect an int (1,2, or 3 indicating bass, mid, treble to control color of the object).  Lastly I'll take two parameters (may be 1,2, or 3) to control the size, second to control x-y distortion.
I'm planning on having a bunch of ellipses that will have variable size, color, and semi-major to major axis ratio.  So the call to my function will be ellipseScene(int bass, int mid, int treble, int color, int size, int ratio).  Note that the last three inputs may have the same value or all different.
Let me know if you guys have any questions for implementing the ui/test cases for my portion.

ID:687379038_577648442318880
Name:null
Story:N/A
Message:I think I'm going to email stotts this tomorrow and say that these are the requirements/use cases we came up with.  If any of you have anything to add or change let me know.  Also, I said mov file since maya doesn't have an avi file format for rendering in mac for some reason. If one of the windows people can let me know if the mov file format is available in windows that would be great.  I also think the 72 hours thing is not going to happen from what I can tell it takes forever to render videos.

Requirements

Tier 1:
 The plugin must run in Maya versions 2014 and 2013.
 The plugin must allow a user to choose an mp3 file to use as the audio source.
 The plugin must produce a video with format mov the Quicktime format.
 The plugin must present a GUI for the user to choose mp3 file as well as save  location for the mov file.

Tier 2:
 The plugin must allow for a user to choose different ?classes? of animation, such  as a group of spheres, a plane of water, or a single ?spiky? sphere.
 The plugin must allow for the user to view a ?rough? rendering of the video in the  viewport in real time.

Tier 3:
 The plugin must allow for the user to choose which audio aspects control certain  visual properties.
 The plugin must allow for different strengths of audio aspects to contribute to  its corresponding visual property.
 The plugin must render a final video in 72 hours time.

Use Cases:

As a user, I want to be able to choose which song to play and have coupled with visualization.

As a user I want to be able to choose which type of visualization is shown.

As a user I want a final video file to be produced once parameters are chosen and decided to be rendered.

As a user I want to be able to see a "rough demo" within the viewport in real time.

As a user I want to be able to decide which audio properties control which visualization properties.

ID:708705302_10152032127220303
Name:null
Story:N/A
Message:Today i walked into Teague and saw all the empty rooms and halls. I felt empty. Today was graduation. It's suppose to be a happy day, but somehow i felt sad.   I walked out of the global center after the econ commencement in a hurry without really saying good byes to my friends because i was tired. I didnt realize that this is one of the last few moments we will have together. In a couple of days, we would all depart. Although we all say "keep in touch" and "visit each other often", the ugly truth is that we probably wont. Its not that we dont value our friendship. Its that we are now going into the real world to start our new life and family, and itll be hard to sit back, relax, and reconnect with our old friends from our busy lives.  Throughout these four years, i made some great friends; some with annoying qualities haha. But today, when its time to depart, all i see and remember are the good times we had together, because thats wut really matters.  This last senior year has been crazy. I had so much fun! Thanks guys for a great year! These are the best times i had on college. I really hope that these days can last forever where we just drink and play random games. Thanks guys! Im not gonna wish u guys good luck for ur post graduation lives because i know you guys wont need it. Im gonna wish for us to be able to come back and relive our days together soon! <3

ID:829326037_10152696713251038
Name:null
Story:N/A
Message:Prior to the start of this basketball season, I wasn't a sports fan in any sense of the word. I didn't grow up watching Carolina on TV. I knew Michael Jordan played here, but that was about it. I had been to one basketball game in my college career, and it was only a non-conference game. I could name one or two starters from the past few years, and certainly couldn't tell you our starting line-up if you had asked me in November.

For the longest time, I couldn't understand why people cared so much about Carolina basketball. I couldn't see why anyone would stand in the freezing cold for hours on end to get a chance to stand on the risers for the entire game. It didn't make sense why everyone got so passionate about a bunch of guys putting a little ball through a hoop.

But then something changed. I don't know what did it, but I started waiting in line for games. I stood in the risers for the first time. I read article after article on ESPN about our team. I bought a #5 jersey. I followed our team when we beat Kentucky and Michigan State, and then I wondered if we would find a way to keep going once the whole PJ thing was over. And, like many of you, I wasn't sure if we'd be able to come back after the 1-4 start in January.

And like many of you... I started believing. I watched with amazement as our team... the team that so many of us almost wrote off at the beginning of the season... the team that struggled with free throws throughout the season... the team that beat Top 10 teams but lost to unranked teams... I watched as this team fought harder than anyone else and won game after game in remarkable fashion over these last few months.

With each game, I believed in this team more and more. I believed when Marcus hit that game-winning lay-up against NC State in February. I believed when Wade hit the three-pointer that put us up over 100 points against Wake to the sound of an ecstatic Smith Center chanting, "Biscuits! Biscuits!" I believed when I went back and watched Roy's post-game interviews after the hard losses as he took responsibility and pledged to the Carolina family that he would do all he could to turn the team around.

I believed when I rushed Franklin Street for the first time in my college career with my closest friends after THIS team beat a better-than-ever Duke line-up in the Dean Dome after being delayed because of the snow.

It was THIS team... Not the fierce '11-'12 or '12-'13 teams... that made this happen. THIS team was the one that offered me one of the most incredible memories of my time at Carolina.

It was THIS team that not only endured, but overcame tremendous opposition from every side and turned themselves around to become a Top 15 team at the close of the season.

It was THIS team that refused to go down without a fight, showing up at every game with a fierce sense of competitiveness and drive that made them so exciting and wonderfully entertaining to watch.

Though I'm not sure how this team will be remembered in the history of Carolina basketball, I know how I will remember it: THIS team was the one that converted me from a stubborn observer on the sideline of college sports into an obsessed fanatic who simply can't get enough of it.

So to Roy, Nate, Leslie, Kennedy, Luke, Marcus, Brice, J.P., Desmond, Jackson, Isaiah, James, Denzel, Joel, James Michael and Wade... I want to say thank-you.

Thank you for this season.
Thank you for fighting.
Thank you for refusing to quit when success seemed impossible.
Thank you for not listening to the doubters and naysayers.
Thank you for making this season something I will undoubtedly remember for the rest of my life.

We love you guys so much, and we will be standing with you next season, the season after, and every single season for the rest of our lives.

Thank you for making me prouder than ever to be a Tar Heel.

THIS IS CAROLINA BASKETBALL!

ID:1149833760_10203878013127958
Name:CET Janterm/Spring 2014
Story:N/A
Message:https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Rb5BSCPli6k

After about a month living in China, I realized that my camera had this really cool feature on it that was able to take photos and videos SIMULTANEOUSLY. Thus, during my travels, explorations, and adventures, I was able to capture a lot of precious memories.

Sometimes, photos can't always tell the full story. Granted, nothing can really take the place of the actual experience. However, with these little snapshots, I was able to capture the little moments right before the click of the shutter - sometimes I got a video of somebody dancing, or a face popping in and disappearing right before a click, or a switch of a facial expression. So, here's my video of all these little clips and other recordings that i've collected, and I hope that everyone can get a real taste of my semester abroad!

To my CET family: look out for yourself in the video! :)
Also --view in full screen!

Message:I was suggested to read a book "Confessions of a Medical Heretic" by M.D. Robert S. Mendelsohn. Here's a part of Stephen Pletko's comment on Amazon: 

Each chapter (there are nine) of this book has many truths. These truths are not out-of-date and will probably remain relevant into the far future. Here are just three examples:

1) "Every drug stresses and hurts your body in some way."
2) "A healthy society is characterized by strong, positive family relationships and subsequent minimal need of doctors."
3) "Doctors are not trained to attack the core of any problem, merely to suppress symptoms."

I am so glad to see that UNC has this book in its library.

Message:ESPN rates Coach K No. 4 best men's college basketball coach in recent years. Here are some interesting stats: Since 2006-07, Duke has won just 1 regular season ACC title. In 6 of those 8 seasons, Duke failed to progress past the Sweet 16. In 3 of those 6 seasons, they lost their 1st NCAA tournament game. In 2 of the last 3 years, they've been sent home right away, by a No. 15 and No. 14 seed, respectively. But, from Nov. 26, 2007, to Jan. 6, 2014, Duke never once ranked outside the Associated Press top 10. The Blue Devils spent 122 straight weeks without falling below No.10, the longest streak since Wooden's UCLA Bruins from 1966-1976. They won it all in 2010. Those stats epitomize Duke in my recent memory.

Name:24 Photos Of China's Insanely Stressful College Entrance Exam Process
Story:N/A
Message:Saw the same Chemistry textbook when I was studying for the exam many years ago. 

Fairly speaking, the exam looks stressful but not too bad. Like any standardized test, there is a quite clear syllabus to specify what will be covered. Each test question is well-defined and ensure you can reach the *correct* answer in minutes if you follow the *expected* thinking process. In contrast, I spent lots of time resolving ambiguities in question when I study in US colleges. In general, it's an amplitude test. Although there are fact-memorization questions, the preparation time is more than enough to get the credit. 

It emphasizes connections between knowledges and test writes are trained to design so, although they are quite artificial and contrived from the view of a college student. The competition makes it like a sport. Some of the specialized skills are quite hard to acquire, and they vary from year to year. Not a bad thing actually, since it's futile to put efforts into the parts where I may never work out timely. Following the school schedule, the performance goes steady smoothly, like doing sports. Therefore, there is nothing much to worry about for the performance for the exam. 

What really bothers is the college application process. For each tier of universities, the number a student may file applications in total is limited (only one in my time). Therefore, it takes risks to plan the overall application. There is no such a thing as multiple offers in the admission system.

Message:IWS & IWR (US Russell Mid-Cap Value) - Buy
We decided to continue hold IWS as part of our long-term strategy. We believe investors will seek these equities once the market pullback stops. We made these trades as a contrarian play for above average return. Even with the murky job reports, consumer services are improving with the report two weeks ago and recent news, making US equities attractive.

EEM, ACWI, EWG, & IOO (Emerging Markets) - Buy
We decided to buy emerging markets due to their heavier weight on tech and financial services aboard. These sectors have done well lately as investors are beginning to stray away from US equity and more into foreign investments.

Message:Macro-economic Outlook
Domestic and International

For this week, the economic calendar reports on S&P Case-Shiller HPI, New Home Sales, Consumer Confidence, Durable Goods Orders, Pending Home Sales Index, Consumer Sentiment, Personal Income and Outlays, and GDP.

Although equities ended on a positive note last week, our team evaluated our current holdings and closed the positions that looked susceptible to increasing volatility and swings within the markets.  Today, we entered new positions that were more conservative and protected against heavy losses. These positions have significantly limited the downturn that is happening in equities.  

Although we have a positive outlook for the economy, most investors are overreacting, and their fears are driving momentum towards these ups and downs.  Our team believes that the economy is improving and the economic indicators show it.  Therefore, we have temporarily entered positions in alternative investments, emerging market investments, long-term bonds, and midcap value stocks.  Equities will improve once positive numbers on GDP and other indicators come out this week.  Then, we will re-apply an aggressive allocation investment strategy as soon as investors begin to realize that they were wrong about their economic outlook.  

The Ukraine crisis, FOMC announcement, and China?s problems have caused uncertainty regarding the recovery.  As the Russian economy continues to be downgraded as an emerging market, foreign investment will focus on frontier markets instead of BRIC countries and limit exposure to the Ukraine Crisis and Putin's legacy, such as the annexation of Crimea and announcement of suspending Russia from the G-7 summit.

ID:100000291936863_784277821591942
Name:null
Story:N/A
Message:Today i walked into Teague and saw all the empty rooms and halls. I felt empty. Today was graduation. It's suppose to be a happy day, but somehow i felt sad.   I walked out of the global center after the econ commencement in a hurry without really saying good byes to my friends because i was tired. I didnt realize that this is one of the last few moments we will have together. In a couple of days, we would all depart. Although we all say "keep in touch" and "visit each other often", the ugly truth is that we probably wont. Its not that we dont value our friendship. Its that we are now going into the real world to start our new life and family, and itll be hard to sit back, relax, and reconnect with our old friends from our busy lives.  Throughout these four years, i made some great friends; some with annoying qualities haha. But today, when its time to depart, all i see and remember are the good times we had together, because thats wut really matters.  This last senior year has been crazy. I had so much fun! Thanks guys for a great year! These are the best times i had on college. I really hope that these days can last forever where we just drink and play random games. Thanks guys! Im not gonna wish u guys good luck for ur post graduation lives because i know you guys wont need it. Im gonna wish for us to be able to come back and relive our days together soon! <3

So my first few days on campus, (I come from a very small town) I was overwhelmed the first few days and I didn?t know that many people. So I ate alone a lot during the first few weeks. One day I was sitting down for lunch at Rams and across from me there is another student. As I sat down, the person across from me asked if I wanted to sit with him. Three years later, he is one of my best friends and he is my campaign manager." One of my favorite Carolina memories!

Story:N/A
Message:Today i walked into Teague and saw all the empty rooms and halls. I felt empty. Today was graduation. It's suppose to be a happy day, but somehow i felt sad.   I walked out of the global center after the econ commencement in a hurry without really saying good byes to my friends because i was tired. I didnt realize that this is one of the last few moments we will have together. In a couple of days, we would all depart. Although we all say "keep in touch" and "visit each other often", the ugly truth is that we probably wont. Its not that we dont value our friendship. Its that we are now going into the real world to start our new life and family, and itll be hard to sit back, relax, and reconnect with our old friends from our busy lives.  Throughout these four years, i made some great friends; some with annoying qualities haha. But today, when its time to depart, all i see and remember are the good times we had together, because thats wut really matters.  This last senior year has been crazy. I had so much fun! Thanks guys for a great year! These are the best times i had on college. I really hope that these days can last forever where we just drink and play random games. Thanks guys! Im not gonna wish u guys good luck for ur post graduation lives because i know you guys wont need it. Im gonna wish for us to be able to come back and relive our days together soon! <3
